# ============================================================================
# CHAOS REDUX - EVENT 005 SOVIET COLLAPSE EFFECTS
# ============================================================================
# This file owns the clean Soviet Collapse crisis scaffold: opening pressure
# setup, breakaway support, crisis-meter arithmetic, and the Soviet objective
# board activation queue. Event stages use these effects; evolutions remain
# separate mutation tracks and are not represented here as stage logs.
# ============================================================================

@soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown_days = 30

soviet_collapse_clamp_crisis_components = {
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_evolution_weirdness min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
}

soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = {
	soviet_collapse_clamp_crisis_components = yes
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_evolution_weirdness }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_offset }
	subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority }
	subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_military_obedience }
	multiply_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_multiplier }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_floor max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_super_event_union_unmade_fired }
		}
		soviet_collapse_show_union_unmade_super_event = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_register_monthly_threat_success = {
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives = 1 }
}

soviet_collapse_register_monthly_threat_failure = {
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives = 1 }
}

soviet_collapse_apply_monthly_threat_guard = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat }

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_war = no
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.success_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.foreign_appetite compare = less_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.league_cohesion compare = less_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_month_cap compare = greater_than }
		}
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_month_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_floor max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_war = no
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.success_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.foreign_appetite compare = less_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.league_cohesion compare = less_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_month_cap compare = greater_than }
		}
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_month_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_floor max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling }
	}

	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives = 0 }
}

soviet_collapse_initialize_mission_requirements = {
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_equipment_req = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.equipment_req }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_support_equipment_req = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.support_equipment_req }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_train_req = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.train_req }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_fuel_req = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.fuel_req }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_manpower_req = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.manpower_req }
}

soviet_collapse_initialize_crisis_values = {
	set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_active
	set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active
	set_global_flag = {
		flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock
		days = 31
	}
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_center
	add_ideas = soviet_collapse_union_crisis

	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.moscow_authority }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.republic_confidence }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.military_obedience }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.depot_vulnerability }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.foreign_appetite }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.league_cohesion }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_evolution_weirdness = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.evolution_weirdness }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = 0 }
	clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries
	clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics

	soviet_collapse_initialize_mission_requirements = yes

	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 1 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_1 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_2 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_2 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_2_foreign_appetite }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_3 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_3 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_3_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_evolution_weirdness = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_3_weirdness }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_4 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_4 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_4_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_evolution_weirdness = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_4_weirdness }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_final }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_final }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_final_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_evolution_weirdness = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_final_weirdness }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_stability < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.good_stability }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.low_stability }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.low_stability_authority }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_support < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.good_war_support }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.low_war_support_obedience }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.low_war_support }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war = yes }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.active_war }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.active_war }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { capital_scope = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.capital_lost_authority }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.capital_lost }
	}

	soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives = 0 }
	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.129 days = 30 }
}

	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_objective_pressure.settlement_success_foreign }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_objective_pressure.settlement_success_league }
	soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
}

soviet_collapse_spawn_loyalist_militias = {
	division_template = {
		name = "Emergency Loyalist Militia"
		is_locked = yes
		force_allow_recruiting = yes
		regiments = {
			infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
			infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_loyalist_militia_count = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.loyalist_militia_unit_count }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Emergency Loyalist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
					owner = PREV
					count = [UNIT_COUNT]
				}
			}
		}
		UNIT_COUNT = "[?soviet_collapse_loyalist_militia_count|.0]"
	}
}

soviet_collapse_emit_super_event = {
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_global_flag = {
				flag = super_event_visible
				days = 30
				value = [SUPER_EVENT_ID]
			}
		}
		SUPER_EVENT_ID = "[?soviet_collapse_super_event_id|.0]"
	}
	set_variable = { global.current_super_event_audio_id = soviet_collapse_super_event_id }
	every_country = {
		limit = { is_ai = no }
		play_current_super_event_audio = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_show_union_unmade_super_event = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_super_event_union_unmade_fired } }
		set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_super_event_union_unmade_fired
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { exists = yes } }
			SOV = { soviet_collapse_apply_terminal_collapse = yes }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_super_event_id = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade }
		soviet_collapse_emit_super_event = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_maybe_show_union_unmade_super_event = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_super_event_union_unmade_fired }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock }
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.min_breakaways_for_union_unmade
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_high_threat
						compare = greater_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_critical_authority
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_contested_authority
						compare = less_than
					}
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_announced
						has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_first_wave_failed
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.deep_collapse_threat
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
			}
		}
		soviet_collapse_show_union_unmade_super_event = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_release_terminal_ordinary_republics = {
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			exists = no
			OR = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = BLR
				tag = MOL
				tag = LIT
				tag = LAT
				tag = EST
				tag = GEO
				tag = ARM
				tag = AZR
				tag = UZB
				tag = KYR
				tag = TAJ
				tag = TMS
			}
			any_state = {
				is_core_of = PREV
				is_owned_by = SOV
				is_controlled_by = SOV
			}
		}
		SOV = { release = PREV }
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
			}
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
			soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
		}
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject_of = SOV
			OR = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = BLR
				tag = MOL
				tag = LIT
				tag = LAT
				tag = EST
				tag = GEO
				tag = ARM
				tag = AZR
				tag = UZB
				tag = KYR
				tag = TAJ
				tag = TMS
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		}
		SOV = { set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free } }
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
		soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			tag = KAZ
			has_soviet_collapse_three_smaller_central_asian_republics_free = yes
			OR = {
				AND = {
					exists = no
					any_state = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						is_owned_by = SOV
						is_controlled_by = SOV
					}
				}
				AND = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = no }
			SOV = { release = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = { set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
			soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_prepare_highest_chaos_terminal_successors = {
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_graves_counted_by_dead_state
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_northern_fleet_signals_unsealed

	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_first_wave_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_loyal_military_districts_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_union_archives_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_grave_registers_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_wrong_resurrection_committee_political
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_ural_factory_gates_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_funeral_train_schedule_survived
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_star_iron_rumor_spread
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_crown_left_archive
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_peasant_anger_joined_green_army
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_villages_negotiation_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_mountain_administration_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_vladivostok_buffer_government_credible
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_siberian_distance_command_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_ural_workers_directorate_declared
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mountain_republic_council_declared
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_idel_ural_league_declared
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_birobidzhan_commune_declared
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_northern_port_directorate_declared
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_religious_command_entered_war_room
	if = {
		limit = {

				var = soviet_collapse_evolution_weirdness
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_weirdness_high
				compare = less_than

		}
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_evolution_weirdness = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_weirdness_high }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_spawn_terminal_high_chaos_successors = {
	soviet_collapse_maybe_spawn_high_chaos_successors = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		soviet_collapse_prepare_highest_chaos_terminal_successors = yes
		soviet_collapse_maybe_spawn_high_chaos_successors = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_terminal_collapse = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse } }
		set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse_in_progress
		soviet_collapse_release_terminal_ordinary_republics = yes
		soviet_collapse_spawn_terminal_high_chaos_successors = yes
		soviet_collapse_cleanup_terminal_collapse_missions = yes
		set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse
		clr_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse_in_progress
		soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway } }
		soviet_collapse_apply_breakaway_setup_package = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_breakaway_setup_package = {
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
	add_to_array = {
		array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries
		value = THIS
	}
	add_to_variable = { global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes } }
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active }
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.first_wave_breakaway_republic_confidence }
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.first_wave_breakaway_depot_vulnerability }
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.first_wave_breakaway_foreign_appetite }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active
					PREV = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes }
				}
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.first_wave_major_republic_confidence }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active
					PREV = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_regional_target = yes }
				}
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.first_wave_regional_republic_confidence }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active }
				soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
			}
			soviet_collapse_maybe_show_union_unmade_super_event = yes
		}
	}

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.base_manpower }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.base_infantry_equipment }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.base_support_equipment }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.base_artillery_equipment }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_guard_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.base_guard_units }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.base_field_units }

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = KAZ
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.major_manpower_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.major_infantry_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.major_support_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.major_artillery_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_guard_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.major_guard_units_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.major_field_units_bonus }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = BLR
				tag = GEO
				tag = AZR
				tag = UZB
				tag = LIT
				tag = LAT
				tag = EST
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.regional_manpower_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.regional_infantry_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.regional_support_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.regional_artillery_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.regional_field_units_bonus }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_manpower_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_infantry_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_support_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_artillery_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_field_units_per_chaos_band }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_manpower_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_infantry_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_support_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_artillery_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_field_units_per_chaos_band }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_manpower_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_infantry_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_support_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_artillery_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_field_units_per_chaos_band }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_manpower_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_infantry_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_support_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_artillery_equipment_per_chaos_band }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.extra_field_units_per_chaos_band }
	}

	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes has_war = yes } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.soviet_war_manpower_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.soviet_war_infantry_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.soviet_war_support_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.soviet_war_field_units_bonus }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = less_than }
					check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.deep_collapse_threat compare = greater_than }
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.weak_center_manpower_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.weak_center_infantry_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.weak_center_support_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.weak_center_artillery_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.weak_center_field_units_bonus }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.high_depot_vulnerability_gate
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.depot_pressure_manpower_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.depot_pressure_infantry_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.depot_pressure_support_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.depot_pressure_artillery_equipment_bonus }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.high_foreign_appetite_gate
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.foreign_access_manpower_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.foreign_access_infantry_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.foreign_access_support_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.foreign_access_field_units_bonus }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_next_declaration_unarmed } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.preempted_declaration_manpower }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.preempted_declaration_infantry_equipment }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.preempted_declaration_support_equipment }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.preempted_declaration_field_units }
		SOV = { clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_next_declaration_unarmed }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_next_declaration_armed } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.emboldened_declaration_manpower }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.emboldened_declaration_infantry_equipment }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.emboldened_declaration_support_equipment }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.emboldened_declaration_field_units }
		SOV = { clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_next_declaration_armed }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse_in_progress }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.terminal_manpower_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.terminal_infantry_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.terminal_support_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.terminal_artillery_equipment_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_guard_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.terminal_guard_units_bonus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.terminal_field_units_bonus }
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count min = 0 max = 12 }

	add_manpower = var:soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = var:soviet_collapse_breakaway_infantry_equipment_package }
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = var:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support_equipment_package }
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_1 amount = var:soviet_collapse_breakaway_artillery_equipment_package }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_recovery_progress = 0 }
	add_ideas = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder

	division_template = {
		name = "Emergency Republican Guard"
		is_locked = yes
		force_allow_recruiting = yes
		regiments = {
			infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
			infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
		}
	}
	division_template = {
		name = "Emergency Republican Field Brigade"
		is_locked = yes
		force_allow_recruiting = yes
		regiments = {
			infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
			infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
			infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
			infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
			infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
			artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }
		}
	}
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Emergency Republican Guard\" start_experience_factor = 0.15 start_equipment_factor = 0.9"
					owner = PREV
					count = [GUARD_UNIT_COUNT]
				}
			}
		}
		GUARD_UNIT_COUNT = "[?soviet_collapse_breakaway_guard_unit_count|.0]"
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count value = 0 compare = greater_than }
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Emergency Republican Field Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.9"
						owner = PREV
						count = [FIELD_UNIT_COUNT]
					}
				}
			}
			FIELD_UNIT_COUNT = "[?soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count|.0]"
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_check_republic_recovery = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_republic_recovery_progress
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_recovery.partial_recovery
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder
			add_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder_mitigated
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_republic_startup_disorder_mitigated
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder
				has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder_mitigated
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_republic_recovery_progress
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_recovery.recovery_complete
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder } remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder_mitigated } remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder_mitigated }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_emergency_administration_stabilized
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_republic_startup_disorder_resolved
	}
}

soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = {
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_recovery_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_recovery.decision_progress }
	soviet_collapse_check_republic_recovery = yes
}

soviet_collapse_add_republic_focus_recovery_progress = {
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_recovery_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_recovery.focus_progress }
	soviet_collapse_check_republic_recovery = yes
}

	soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes

		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.recognition_soviet_foreign_pressure }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.recognition_soviet_republic_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_breakaway_front_coordination = {
	add_fuel = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.coordinate_fuel_spend
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.coordinate_support_equipment_spend }

		array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries

				exists = yes

			}
			add_ideas = soviet_collapse_defensive_coordination

			soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.coordinate_league_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_influence_delta = {
	FROM = {
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_delta }
	}
	if = { limit = { tag = GER } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_germany = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = ENG } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_britain = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = JAP } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_japan = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = FRA } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_france = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = USA } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_usa = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = TUR } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_turkey = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = PER } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_iran = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = POL } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_poland = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = ROM } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_romania = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = FIN } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_finland = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = SWE } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_sweden = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = ITA } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_italy = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	FROM = { soviet_collapse_update_sponsor_balance_pressure = yes }
}

soviet_collapse_update_sponsor_balance_pressure = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_germany value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_germany value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_germany }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_germany value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_germany }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_britain value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_britain value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_britain }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_britain value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_britain }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_japan value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_japan value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_japan }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_japan value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_japan }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_france value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_france value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_france }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_france value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_france }

	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_italy value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_italy value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_italy }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_italy value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_italy }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_gap = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_gap = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence }
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_two_resilience }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_two_patronage_risk }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_three_resilience }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_three_patronage_risk }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_warning }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_warning_influence compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_gap value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_warning_gap compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_warning
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_warning_patronage_risk }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_warning_resilience }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_lock }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_lock_influence compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_gap value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_lock_gap compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_lock
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_lock_patronage_risk }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_lock_resilience }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_update_foreign_investment_stage_ideas = {
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_diplomatic_contacts
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_diplomatic_mission
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_treaty_backing
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_supply_contacts
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_supply_corridors
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_supply_network
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_reconstruction_offers
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_sponsored_civil_works
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_sovereign_reconstruction_board
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_volunteer_cadres
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_volunteer_brigades
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_international_defense_corps
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_military_observers
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_training_mission
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_joint_staff_mission
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_contacts
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_liaison
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_network
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_recognition_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_3_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_treaty_backing
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_recognition_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_2_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_diplomatic_mission
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_recognition_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_1_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_diplomatic_contacts
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_material_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_arms_total }
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_material_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_industry_total }
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_material_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_logistics_total }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_material_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_3_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_supply_network
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_material_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_2_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_supply_corridors
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_material_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_1_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_supply_contacts
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_investment_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_industry_total }
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_investment_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_logistics_total }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_investment_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_3_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_sovereign_reconstruction_board
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_investment_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_2_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_sponsored_civil_works
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_investment_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_1_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_reconstruction_offers
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_volunteers_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_3_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_international_defense_corps
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_volunteers_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_2_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_volunteer_brigades
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_volunteers_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_1_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_volunteer_cadres
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_advisers_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_3_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_joint_staff_mission
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_advisers_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_2_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_training_mission
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_advisers_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_1_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_military_observers
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_patron_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_volunteers_total }
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_patron_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_intelligence_total }
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_patron_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_ideology_total }
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_patron_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_patron_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_3_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_network
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_patron_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_2_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_liaison
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_patron_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_1_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_contacts
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_recognition_aid = {
	if = { limit = { has_government = democratic } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_democratic_patron_contest_completed }
	if = { limit = { has_war_with = SOV } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_hostile_patron_double_game }
	add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_stability_spend
	add_war_support = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_war_support_spend
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_regional_target = yes } }
		add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_regional_stability_extra_spend
		add_war_support = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_regional_war_support_extra_spend
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes } }
		add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_major_stability_extra_spend
		add_war_support = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_major_war_support_extra_spend
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.recognition_influence }
	soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_influence_delta = yes
	FROM = {
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_recognition_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_progress }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_recognition_total = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.recognition_influence }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_legal_restoration_claim
		soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes
		soviet_collapse_update_foreign_investment_stage_ideas = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_soviet_foreign_pressure }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_soviet_republic_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_liaison_aid = {
	if = { limit = { has_government = democratic } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_democratic_patron_contest_completed }
	if = { limit = { has_war_with = SOV } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_hostile_patron_double_game }
	add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_stability_spend
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_regional_target = yes } }
		add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_regional_stability_extra_spend
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes } }
		add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_major_stability_extra_spend
	}
	if = { limit = { has_government = communism } FROM = { add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_ideology_popularity } } }
	if = { limit = { has_government = democratic } FROM = { add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_ideology_popularity } } }
	if = { limit = { has_government = fascism } FROM = { add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_ideology_popularity } } }
	if = { limit = { has_government = neutrality } FROM = { add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_ideology_popularity } } }

soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			tag = UKR
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_ukraine_focus_tree }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			tag = BLR
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_belarus_focus_tree }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			tag = KAZ
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_focus_tree }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			OR = {
				tag = LIT
				tag = LAT
				tag = EST
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_baltic_focus_tree }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			OR = {
				tag = GEO
				tag = ARM
				tag = AZR
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_caucasus_focus_tree }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			OR = {
				tag = UZB
				tag = KYR
				tag = TAJ
				tag = TMS
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_central_asia_focus_tree }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			tag = MOL
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_moldova_focus_tree }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = UKR
					tag = BLR
					tag = KAZ
					tag = LIT
					tag = LAT
					tag = EST
					tag = GEO
					tag = ARM
					tag = AZR
					tag = UZB
					tag = KYR
					tag = TAJ
					tag = TMS
					tag = MOL
				}
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_breakaway_focus_tree }
	}
}

	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_member
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_commitments
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_recognition_progress = -1 }

soviet_collapse_call_regional_league_defensive_war = {
	add_command_power = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_command_power_spend
	add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_manpower_spend
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_league_defensive_war_called
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
			can_declare_war_on = SOV
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SOV
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	every_other_country = {
		limit = {
			is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_member = yes
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
		}
		add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_manpower_reward
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_equipment_reward }
		add_to_war = {
			targeted_alliance = ROOT
			enemy = SOV
			hostility_reason = asked_to_join
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.soviet_release_pressure }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.soviet_release_pressure }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.soviet_foreign_pressure }
			clr_global_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
			soviet_collapse_maybe_release_threat_breakaway = yes
		}
	}
	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.43 }
}

	if = { limit = { GEO = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } add_to_faction = GEO GEO = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_member add_ideas = soviet_collapse_defensive_coordination } }
	if = { limit = { ARM = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } add_to_faction = ARM ARM = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_member add_ideas = soviet_collapse_defensive_coordination } }
	if = { limit = { AZR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } add_to_faction = AZR AZR = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_member add_ideas = soviet_collapse_defensive_coordination } }
	if = { limit = { MOL = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } add_to_faction = MOL MOL = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_member add_ideas = soviet_collapse_defensive_coordination } }
	if = { limit = { UZB = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } add_to_faction = UZB UZB = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_member add_ideas = soviet_collapse_defensive_coordination } }
	if = { limit = { KYR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } add_to_faction = KYR KYR = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_member add_ideas = soviet_collapse_defensive_coordination } }

	soviet_collapse_apply_focus_league_preparation = yes

			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes

soviet_collapse_record_high_chaos_successor_evolution = {
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_event_id = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.event_id }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.evolution_type }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.totalen_tier }
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.world_collapse_tier }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { can_soviet_collapse_record_high_chaos_evolution_this_tier = yes }
		save_event_target_as = events_log_evolution_actor
		record_events_log_evolution_entry = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_evolution_tier_5_recorded
		}
		else = {
			set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_evolution_tier_4_recorded
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_setup_cfr_successor = {
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_factory_successor
	set_capital = {
		state = 248
		remember_old_capital = no
	}
	soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
	load_focus_tree = { tree = CFR_soviet_collapse_focus_tree keep_completed = no }
	set_variable = { cfr_construction_mandates = constant:soviet_collapse_factory_ancient.medium_mandate_gain }
	add_ideas = cfr_construction_mandates
	add_ideas = cfr_housing_ration_boards
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_stage = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.civilian_factory_stage }
	soviet_collapse_record_high_chaos_successor_evolution = yes
	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5_factory_ancient.1 hours = 6 }
}

	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5_custom.33 hours = 20 }
}

soviet_collapse_add_random_first_wave_western_republic = {
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = BLR
				tag = MOL
				tag = LIT
				tag = LAT
				tag = EST
			}
			NOT = { is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics value = THIS } }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					exists = no
					any_state = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						is_owned_by = SOV
						is_controlled_by = SOV
					}
				}
				AND = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		random_select_amount = 1
		add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics value = THIS }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_add_random_first_wave_caucasus_republic = {
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = GEO
				tag = ARM
				tag = AZR
			}
			NOT = { is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics value = THIS } }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					exists = no
					any_state = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						is_owned_by = SOV
						is_controlled_by = SOV
					}
				}
				AND = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		random_select_amount = 1
		add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics value = THIS }
	}
}
