soviet_collapse_release_one_threat_breakaway_republic = {
	clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics
	soviet_collapse_add_random_threat_breakaway_republic = yes
	soviet_collapse_release_selected_first_wave_republics = yes
	clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown_days = @soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown_days }
	set_global_flag = {
		flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown
		days = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown_days
	}
}

soviet_collapse_fire_progressive_release_event = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_ministry_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_ministry_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_rail_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_rail_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_border_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_border_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_party_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_party_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_foreign_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_foreign_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_depot_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_depot_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_old_movement_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_old_movement_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_league_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_league_weight }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.foreign_appetite compare = less_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_foreign_weight = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.depot_vulnerability compare = less_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_depot_weight = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_evolution_weirdness value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.evolution_weirdness compare = less_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_old_movement_weight = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_league_pressure_ready = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.league_cohesion compare = less_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_league_weight = 0 }
	}
	random_list = {
		var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_ministry_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.130 } }
		var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_rail_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.131 } }
		var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_border_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.132 } }
		var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_party_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.133 } }
		var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_foreign_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.134 } }
		var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_depot_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.135 } }
		var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_old_movement_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.136 } }
		var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_league_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.137 } }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_maybe_release_threat_breakaway = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown }
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.low_threat
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			soviet_collapse_show_union_unmade_super_event = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = mtth:soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight }
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight = mtth:soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight }
			random_list = {
				var:soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = { soviet_collapse_fire_progressive_release_event = yes }
				var:soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight = { }
			}
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_release_selected_first_wave_republics = {
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics
		if = {
			limit = { exists = no }
			SOV = { release = PREV }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = { set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free } }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
			soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_release_initial_republics = {
	clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics

	soviet_collapse_add_random_first_wave_western_republic = yes
	soviet_collapse_add_random_first_wave_caucasus_republic = yes
	soviet_collapse_add_random_first_wave_central_asian_republic = yes

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				AND = {
					has_war = yes
					OR = {
						has_stability < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.good_stability
						has_war_support < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.good_war_support
					}
				}
			}
		}
		soviet_collapse_add_random_extra_first_wave_republic = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				AND = {
					has_war = yes
					has_stability < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.min_stability
				}
			}
		}
		soviet_collapse_add_random_extra_first_wave_republic = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		soviet_collapse_add_random_extra_first_wave_republic = yes
	}

	soviet_collapse_release_selected_first_wave_republics = yes

	if = {
		limit = { can_soviet_collapse_open_kazakhstan_first_wave = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { KAZ = { exists = no } }
			release = KAZ
			KAZ = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { KAZ = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV } }
			set_autonomy = { target = KAZ autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			KAZ = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic }
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			KAZ = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			}
		}
		KAZ = { soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { UZB = { exists = no } }
			release = UZB
			UZB = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { UZB = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV } }
			set_autonomy = { target = UZB autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			UZB = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				}
				KYR = { exists = no }
			}
			release = KYR
			KYR = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				}
				KYR = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV }
			}
			set_autonomy = { target = KYR autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			KYR = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				}
				TAJ = { exists = no }
			}
			release = TAJ
			TAJ = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				}
				TAJ = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV }
			}
			set_autonomy = { target = TAJ autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			TAJ = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				TMS = { exists = no }
			}
			release = TMS
			TMS = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				TMS = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV }
			}
			set_autonomy = { target = TMS autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			TMS = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
		}
	}

	if = { limit = { UKR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } UKR = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { BLR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } BLR = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { KAZ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } KAZ = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { UZB = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } UZB = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { KYR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } KYR = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { TAJ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } TAJ = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { TMS = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } TMS = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	soviet_collapse_maybe_spawn_high_chaos_successors = yes
	clr_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active
}

soviet_collapse_activate_opening_objectives = {
	soviet_collapse_count_active_soviet_objectives = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objectives = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.active_cap }
	}
	soviet_collapse_maybe_release_threat_breakaway = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objectives = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.active_cap }
	}

	if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_active_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.active_cap compare = less_than } NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_001_done } NOT = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_001_confirm_the_emergency_chain_of_command } } activate_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_001_confirm_the_emergency_chain_of_command add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objectives = 1 } }
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_active_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.active_cap compare = less_than } NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_002_done } NOT = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_002_seal_the_first_circular } } activate_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_002_seal_the_first_circular add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objectives = 1 } }
